<username>Al Zirino<//username><Date>1454866710910< /Date>< rating>
5< /rating>
< review>
Meanley's is a wonderful store in the center of La Jolla where one can find most of the practical things needed around the home or garden: paint, nails, screws, tools, hardware, electrical materials, Swiss army knives, cooking pots, cleaning supplies, mouse traps, etc.  The store is of modest size but their inventory is huge, and 95% of the time, one finds what one needs.  Probably the best part, though, is that you don't need to search by yourself.  The store's staff is very friendly and  incredibly helpful, especially with sage advice, which is worth a trip to the store by itself.  This store is a gem on Girard!</review>

<Time>1614971708653</Time><user_id>117979874712714491862< /user_id>< Review>
I just order two meals and beverages from Wahoo's Fish Tacos on Camino Los Mares with Door Dash.

When the driver was approaching the house I could see he was carrying only one beverage. I asked him where other drink was at and he said the Wahoo's employee said everything was there.

I checked the bag and thought I saw it, but was only the lid to the salsa.

I called the restaurant and the employee that answered the phone said I got my drink, accused me of lying, and said I was a bad customer.

I asked to speak with a manager and he told that there wasn't one. When I pressed for the managers name he then said he was the manager. I then asked what his name was and he said Chris. I assumed he was lying to me again and asked him if he was. He told me he was lying about his name too.

I acknowledged that mistakes happen all the time with delivery orders. His response was "then why would ever order take out"? I told this was worst customer service I have ever received and he again called me a bad customer.

We have dined at this Wahoo's location several times and never received such horrible customer service. I plan on sharing this regretful experience with the real manager once I learn who that is with the hope that they can correct the problem for future patrons.

We will not be visiting this restaurant ever again. I still can't believe I was accused of lying about receiving a $2.30 iced tea. I tried to explain to the very rude employee that I wouldn't have even called if the order had been delivered correctly.

Wahoo's just lost a local family as a customer over an iced tea. I will share this on the Next Door app and with all our neighbors.< /Review>
